<p>Originated 1890–95 <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">חֻצְפָּה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>Ultimately</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aramaic" class="extiw" title="w:Aramaic">Aramaic</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="arc">חוצפא</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="arc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr ***ciao.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ciao.html>ciao</a> (10126)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Venetian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Venetian language">Venetian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="vec">s-ciao</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="vec">sciavo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:slave.html>slave</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:particular.html>particular</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:expression.html>expression</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="vec">s-ciao vostro</i>, literally <a href = vnd.unilang:meaning.html>meaning</a> "(<a href = vnd.unilang:i.html>I</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:am.html>am</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:your.html>your</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slave.html>slave</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:but.html>but</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:essence.html>essence</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meaning.html>meaning</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:i.html>I</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:am.html>am</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:your.html>your</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:service.html>service</a>", <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:your.html>your</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:humble.html>humble</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:servant.html>servant</a>"), <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval <a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sclavus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:slave.html>slave</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (whence <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:standard.html>standard</a> Italian <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">schiavo</i>); <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> Venetian <a href = vnd.unilang:language.html>language</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:originally.html>originally</a> pronounced <span class="IPA">/stʃaʊ/</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:development.html>Development</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:use.html>use</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:similar.html>similar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:southern.html>Southern</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:central.html>Central</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:european.html>European</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greeting.html>greeting</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">servus</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cimbaal.html>cimbaal</a> (118795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">simbale</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">cimbale</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cymbalum</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κύμβαλον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúmbalon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:variant.html>variant</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:that.html>that</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a>.
